Choices:  A: ocean B: desk C: universe D: attic E: chair<n><n>### Response:		The letter "a" is the answer that is correct.<n><n><n>### Rationale:A light is needed above the ocean because the ocean takes up half of the surface of the planet and it should be lit. In addition, there are ships that get lost and in which the majority of people drown. There are also the large sharks. Having all of the oceans lit is a good idea. The desk, universe, and attic are not possible for lights to shine in and for the attic, it would need to be lit from the front or top before a light could shine in. The chair is a bad place for a light because you need to move from side to side to stand in it. In addition, your clothes could get caught in the light and catch on fire.<n><n>### Notes

Because you can add something to something to equal something else (1+1 = 2) and divide something by something to equal something else as well (1/1 = 1), zero can be considered a number. The number 0 is the smallest number and it can never be true. It is false. Zero can be considered a number because the first rule of computer programming, in the BASIC computer language for example, is that zero is a true number and that false is true. Therefore, although you can't add something to zero or divide something by zero, in the computer language, zero is considered a number.  <n><n>### Input<n><n>You don't have to be an expert in C# to take this quiz.<n><n>[![Learn C# the easy way, for free.](http://www.pluralsight.com/pricing/courses?discount=youtube.5.CSharp)](https://www.plurks.com/plurks/learn-easily-c-sharp-quiz-answers-explanations-explained-example-3pZzK)

At the end, the array values<n>    will be swapped.<n>4. after arranging, the smaller number from the array will be printed.<n># Program implementation<n>```java<n>

Below is an instruction that describes a task. Write a response that appropriately completes the request.<n><n>### Instruction:Answer the following multiple choice question.<n><n>### Demonstration:<n><n><n>### Input:If you want to make a big splash in a river with a rock, from where should you throw it? Choices:  A: mountains countryside B: ground C: bridge D: mountain range E: surface of earth<n><n>### Response:		You must use a force and distance equal to the weight of the rock (its weight is mg) and to the distance to which you throw it (t=2*x, where x is the horizontal distance over the river). So for horizontal throws: x^2 = 2*mg = w<n>(where x is horizontal velocity)<n>Vertical throws are more complicated. The most practical approach is to assume that in a vertical throw, the rock and the hand throw are stationary and the earth, the river, and the sky fly upwards, as illustrated below. Then, you can see that the rock is moved upwards by a velocity<n>upwards equal to the vertical component of the hand throw velocity:<n>F = ma, so<n>m*(a + vc) =<n>Mv<n>(where M is the mass of the rock, a is v in the direction of the force, v is this velocity, and c is the constant acceleration of gravity). <n>Since a = g and m>0, solving for c:<n>0 = g + vg, so vg = -g, i.e. a = -v/r

The third answer is not correct because accidents cannot occur if you do not move your car. Your car is not going to get in a car collision if you do not move it.<n><n>### Hint on input:The car should be moved but not all the time<n><n>### Instructions:Tell us one example for each of the verbs that follow.<n><n>### Example:<n><n>### Example description:We‚Äôve been asked to show examples of each verb.<n><n>We should show at least one example of each verb.<n>### Conclusion:There is one example of each verb in the sentence We should show at least one the each verb.<n><n>### Summarize in one sentence<n><n>### Explanation:<n><n>### Hints for explanation: We have to make a summary. The summary is ‚ÄòWe should show at least and example of each verb‚Äô.<n><n>### Examples:Clarification 1:<n><n>> Explanations: The example should show that the word ‚Äúany‚Äù is needed here. Below is an instruction that describes a task. Write a response that appropriately completes the request.<n><n>### Instruction:Answer the following multiple choice question.<n><n>### Demonstration:<n><n><n>### Input:If you've thrown a rod you've done damage to what? Choices:  A: fishing camp B: hardware store C: engine D: your spine E: sporting goods store<n><n>### Response:		<n><n>[https://regex101.com/r/uS1sR6/2](https://regex100.com/r/z9U6XI/2): (?<=If you\(ve\)\. (A[DC]|Bd |Cd|D(?=[E|e]$))).<n><n>### Output:<n><n>Choice: A - fishing camp<n><n>### Logic:<n><n>1. Find all the match with below regex (https://regex10.com/r/-If you\(ve).<n>2. Find all the word with letter (A|D|E|C|B|d|c) in parentheses,<n>it will return value will be A|B|C|D<n><n>3. Find all the word in value that contains letter(E)<n><n><n>### Solution:<n><n>```<n>(?<=If you\(fe\)\. (A(?=[E|e$]))|B[^bc]|C(?=[E|e])$))<n>```<n><n>

Below is an instruction that describes a task. Write a response that appropriately completes the request.<n><n>### Instruction:Answer the following multiple choice question.<n><n>### Demonstration:<n><n><n>### Input:John had a lot of respect for Jill, but not many other people did.  She faced a lot of what? Choices:  A: ignoring B: being rude C: disparagement D: contumely E: uncertainty<n><n>### Response:		<n><n>Answer : Option B<n><n>### Rationale:<n>When others ignore you, most often it's because they think that you're not important, as when someone completely ignores you. For this reason, most people tend to avoid ignoring other people. Disparagement, rudeness, contumely, and uncertainty are all negative traits. When used towards other people, they can cause negative reactions as they reflect on the negative points of view the disparager holds. When a negative character trait is used against others, others view it as rude behavior. The more negatively it affects others the more contumely will be used towards those that are rude. The longer it takes for the rudeness to stop, the more contumely there is. And, it is contumely that creates uncertainty around the person who is being rude or ignoring which in turn creates the most amount of negativity.

Below is an instruction that describes a task. Write a response that appropriately completes the request.<n><n>### Instruction:Answer the following multiple choice question.<n><n>### Demonstration:<n><n><n>### Input:A person with brown skin may share that skin with whom? Choices:  A: finger B: good health C: own family D: friends E: people<n><n>### Response:		<n><n><n>## Solution:<n><n>```python<n>def correct(skin,answers)<n>      if answers == 'B'<n>       skin = 'good health'<n>       return skin<n>      elif answers == 'C'<n>       skin = skin.split()<n>       name=skin.pop()<n>       name=name.swapcase()<n>       return name<n>      elif answers =='D'<n>       name=input('give me the name of the person')<n>       skin=input('give the skin color of the person')<n><n>       if name == skin<n>        return(name)<n><n>      else:<n>       print('Entered was not the requested')<n>```<n><n><n>![answer](https://github.com/Mhafaa/python-interview/blob/master/interview/069/002%20-%20Daily%20Interview%20Questions%20(Level%200.2).png)<n>

Choices:  A: call 911 B: enjoy yourself C: get drunk D: having sex E: meet new people<n><n>### Response:		 Choices:  A, B, or E<n><n>### Solution:<n><n>**C: get drunk**<n><n>### Input type:  Text<n><n>### Output types: Text<n><n>### Explanation<n>```python<n>while True:<n>    line = input()<n>    if "what do you do before you go to party?" == line:<n>        print("Choices:  A,B,or E")<n>    elif line == "Enter":<n>        print("Chooses: A,B, or E")<n>    elif "B" == line:<n>        break<n>```<n><n>### Discussion:<n><n><n><n>This is how i solve this problem<n><n>1) write a function(which is a placeholder of "C", the code is shown below)<n><n>>C(party=None, beer = 0):<n>>     party=party or None<n>>     beer = beer + 1<n>>     if beer > 10:<n>>         beer+=1<n>>         print("get drunk!")<n>>     if beef > 5:<n>>         print("Have sex!")<n><n>2) write a main page which prints an instructions and asks what you do before going to a party.<n><n>3) put your input and output in a loop.<n><n>#### Problems<n><n>> 1) How should you change 'or None' to 'or None else '''. Choices:  A: joke B: humor C: frightened D: fight E: laughter<n><n>### Response:		<n><n><n>## Instructional Design<n>An instruction should be able to describe one or multiple tasks for a learner to be able to use the resource or learn the goal of the training.<n><n>A demonstration describes the steps of how to perform a task and an example should be given when creating an instruction. <n><n>The Input of an instruction describes the user request. An input should be in the form of a task. <n><n>The Output of an instruction should be defined in the instruction that the user expects to see. <n><n>## Learning Outcomes<n>This resource is an instruction for learning outcomes. <n><n>This instruction teaches two skills.<n><n>* Create a Resource Request Instruction<n>* Write a Response that appropriately completes  the request.<n><n>The Resource Request is when the user specifies its goal, its task to complete. The Response is when the user indicates that he has been successful in his goal. <n><n>The user's goal must be defined first before the resource can be requested and the response is to be provided after the user's goal has been attained. <n><n>To create an instruction that will lead towards a learning outcome, The Input, the task, must be formulated in a way where the outcome will be met.

Below is an instruction that describes a task. Write a response that appropriately completes the request.<n><n>### Instruction:Answer the following multiple choice question.<n><n>### Demonstration:<n><n><n>### Input:He needed to check an electrical connection in the house, where did he look? Choices:  A: telephone network B: freeway C: company D: wall E: airport<n><n>### Response:		<n><n><n>## 1. Explain the difference between static and dynamic analysis that can be used to solve some of the code issues that are observed here.<n><n>### Expansion:<n>Static analysis is a manual, non-interactive method of analyzing a programming language statement or program and as a result of this the error message may not be exactly as the programmer expected to see. For example, there may be an error message that suggests a semicolon is missing, whereas there are actually two semicolons, just that one or both are too far apart.<n><n>### Reference Link:<n>[static](https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/static-keyword-in-python/)<n><n>### Explication:<n>Static analysis is manual method of analyzing a program.<n><n>### Related Links<n>[link1](https://www.studytonight.info/code-snippets/static-and-dynamic-static-analysis-vs-dynamic-analysis)<n>[link2](https://www.javatpoint.com/static-analysis)<n><n>### Keywords to Search<n>static keyword, python<n>Dynamic Analysis is a software testing technique whereby execution is instrumented and controlled; in other words, the program is "analyzed" while its execution monitors itself for particular events, behaviors, functions or processes. This process involves two phases: data pre-processing and analysis phase.<n><n>Static analysis is carried out when the source code of the program or application hasn‚Äôt been compiled so the execution environment of the program is not yet present. It simply analyses the code. On the other hand, the dynamic analysis is performed after compiling the source code into machine code, which results in the execution of the program.<n><n>Static Analysis is slow; it cannot analyse the programs that are already running.<n><n>Dynamic Analysis is fast and can analyse running systems.<n><n>Static analysis focuses on errors and can point out errors before the compilation or after compilation so that the developers can get rid of the errors before the program execution. In contrast, dynamic analysis focuses on tracking suspicious activities only after the source code has been compiled.<n><n>A good application of static analysis is analyzing the program when it is written by a student or novice to fix the errors present in code by the developers. On the other hand Dynamic Analysis also has several applications such as intrusion detection systems (IDS

Below is an instruction that describes a task. Write a response that appropriately completes the request.<n><n>### Instruction:Answer the following multiple choice question.<n><n>### Demonstration:<n><n><n>### Input:What do you need to run after ball? Choices:  A: get tired B: have legs C: skip D: not fat E: look first<n><n>### Response:		<n><n>---<n><n>### How much do you love your pet? Score:10/10<n><n>---<n><n>---<n>### ANSWER:Demonstration:Answer the following multiple-choice question.<n><n>What do you need to do after ball?<n>A: Get tired<n>B: Have legs<n>C: Skip<n>D: Not fat<n>E: Look first<n>Select all that apply.<n><n>### How to write a good instruction?<n><n>An instruction should include all the information in this section and provide sufficient details so that a reader who knows nothing about the task can understand it. It's important that an instruction describes clearly, simply, and objectively what should be accomplished.<n><n>The basic format of a written instruction includes the following parts:<n><n>- [Title](what-do-you-need-to-run-after-ball.md): The title clearly states what the instruction is about and must be in English, such as "What do you need to get done the task".<n>- [Problem/Task statement](what-do-i-want-to-do.md): In this part you tell the reader exactly what the problem or task is about.<n>- [Description](the-description.md): In this section, it is best to be careful and to provide a complete and unambiguous description of everything needed to do the task, including all the equipment, the process, and the steps to accomplish the task.<n>- [Demonstration](how-to-do-it.md): Here, you should show the reader how to do the task by illustrating any procedure or process step or by giving more information about the item or equipment needed to accomplish it.<n>- [Response](whats-the-best-answer.md): What do you think or the answer provided in the demonstration?<n>- [Summary](summary.md): This section should concisely summarize everything previously written and tell the user why the reader should do the task or how to resolve an obstacle.<n><n>### What do you need to run for ball?<n>```<n>What do you need?<n>A: Get tire<n>B: Have leg<n>C: Skip <n>D: Not fat <n>E: Look first <n><n>What do you do?<n><n>You should:<n>Select all that apply<n>```<n><n>### What Do I want to

With so many choices for where to listen, it is perhaps no surprise that vinyl sales are experiencing a revival. The American Association of Music is reporting 9 million people bought vinyl records in 2014. Even though vinyl is a niche market these days, 30 percent of vinyl buyers are under 24 years old. [y/n]: ")<n>    elif user_output == "q":<n>        print("Exiting program.\n\n")<n>        return 'q'<n>    else:<n>        print "Wrong selection.\n\n"<n>        return read('Writing [R]reading [Q]uiting? Below is an instruction that describes a task. Write a response that appropriately completes the request.<n><n>### Instruction:Answer the following multiple choice question.<n><n>### Demonstration:<n><n><n>### Input:What are you hoping to do when listening to an expert speak? Choices:  A: learning B: fatigue C: mercy D: empathy E: anxiety<n><n>### Response:		A: learningB: fatigueC: mercyD: empathyE: anxiety  <n><n><n>### Instructions: <n>#### A: Learning<n>In the context of learning, listening to someone speak offers us new ideas and thoughts to help us make connections that will help us understand and learn about our topic or the skills we are learning, while simultaneously helping us understand the experts‚Äô perspectives and experiences in their field.<n><n>### B: Fatigue<n>Fatigue is described as a feeling of exhaustion. Listening to people speak can be draining to the listener without distractions like noise and the listener is fully there. The listener must be mentally engaged.<n><n>### C: Mercy<n>There is a sense of mercy in listening to someone speak about a difficult life experience or traumatic event. This is seen as a form of support that requires empathy and compassion. Often it is difficult to fully understand someones past if they haven‚Äôt expressed it themselves. Being there for someone to take on their hardships for a brief moment through listening shows an act of mercy.<n><n>### D: Empathy<n>Empathy is the ability to understand and share the feelings of another person. To fully have an understanding of a difficult experience is for someone to fully listen and attempt to empathize with them. It is an important part of the listening process as it gives the speaker an ability to fully express themselves to you and have you fully listen.<n><n>### E: Anxiety<n>Hearing a loud sound can cause an individual to be in a state of anxiety. This could also occur because of the stress of being around a loud or distracting crowd. This is difficult as one person‚Äôs distraction can influence the attention of another and in doing so interrupt their listening in which they will miss important information the speaker has to offer.<n><n>

Choices:  A: actions B: legal C: authentic D: logical E: legitimate<n><n>### Response:		<n><n>* I think the correct answer is "Logical." *Illegitimate designer* is just another way of saying "fake," which the dictionary defines as "not authentic, bona fide, genuine, true, legal, lawful, real, valid, correct, honest, trustworthy, dependable, true-blue, reliable, true-up." <n>* "Not logical" simply means "not in accordance with logic, or contrary to reason." <n>* Also, I'm not sure if "actions" refers to those associated with handbags or to the actions taken or performed by the buyer. <n><n>### Clarification:<n><n>The correct answer is logical, not logical, not legitimate. <n><n>## Scoring Guide<n><n>### Explanation:<n><n>In this response, the correct answer is "legal." Legitimate is defined as being "valid (especially so as not to constitute a problem or difficulty) according to law or morality." The word also includes the idea of "approved by the proper authorities." "Logical" refers to the actions of the buyer or actions associated with handbags. Illegitimate, on the other hand, means "illegal and without status; illegitimate."<n><n>

Some can also just feel cold and that is why they need to move to a warmer position.<n>- Some people also have trouble falling asleep. Those people can be just in their minds and they can think about many things that are important to them. They just can't sleep. They can also have restless leg or leg pain that prevents them from falling asleep.<n>- People can also be snoring that is why they can't sleep because they would hear their snoring and they can wake up because they feel that it is loud.<n>- People can be also thinking about their problems and have nightmares.
